1177         \textcolor{comment}{/* Give user a chance to reallocate the stack.  Use copies of}

1321   \textcolor{comment}{/* If YYLEN is nonzero, implement the default value of the action:}
1322 \textcolor{comment}{     '$$ = $1'.}
1323 \textcolor{comment}{}
1324 \textcolor{comment}{     Otherwise, the following line sets YYVAL to garbage.}
1325 \textcolor{comment}{     This behavior is undocumented and Bison}
1326 \textcolor{comment}{     users should not rely upon it.  Assigning to YYVAL}
1327 \textcolor{comment}{     unconditionally makes the parser a bit smaller, and it avoids a}
1328 \textcolor{comment}{     GCC warning that YYVAL may be used uninitialized.  */}

1671   \textcolor{comment}{/* User semantic actions sometimes alter yychar, and that requires}
1672 \textcolor{comment}{     that yytoken be updated with the new translation.  We take the}
1673 \textcolor{comment}{     approach of translating immediately before every use of yytoken.}
1674 \textcolor{comment}{     One alternative is translating here after every semantic action,}
1675 \textcolor{comment}{     but that translation would be missed if the semantic action invokes}
1676 \textcolor{comment}{     YYABORT, YYACCEPT, or YYERROR immediately after altering yychar or}
1677 \textcolor{comment}{     if it invokes YYBACKUP.  In the case of YYABORT or YYACCEPT, an}
1678 \textcolor{comment}{     incorrect destructor might then be invoked immediately.  In the}
1679 \textcolor{comment}{     case of YYERROR or YYBACKUP, subsequent parser actions might lead}
1680 \textcolor{comment}{     to an incorrect destructor call or verbose syntax error message}
1681 \textcolor{comment}{     before the lookahead is translated.  */}

1686   \hyperlink{util__expr__parse_8c_a7a52157fbe194e3a347afc4ef750af77}{YY\_STACK\_PRINT} (yyss, yyssp);

1688   *++yyvsp = yyval;
1689 
1690   \textcolor{comment}{/* Now 'shift' the result of the reduction.  Determine what state}
1691 \textcolor{comment}{     that goes to, based on the state we popped back to and the rule}
1692 \textcolor{comment}{     number reduced by.  */}
1693

1697   \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (0 <= yystate && yystate <= \hyperlink{util__expr__parse_8c_ae67923760a28e3b7ed3aa2cfaef7f9a2}{YYLAST} && yycheck[yystate] == *yyssp)

1699   \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}
